shared_focus = {
	id = AET_anarchy
	icon = GFX_goal_generic_demand_territory
	cost = 5.00
	#prerequisite = { focus = AET_start_focus }
	mutually_exclusive = { focus = AET_realpolitik }
	mutually_exclusive = { focus = AET_archonate_help }
	x = 17
	y = 0
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 200
	}
	allow_branch = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = obsolete_focus_branches_visibility
						option = HIDE
					}
				}
				NOT = {
					OR = {
						has_completed_focus = AET_realpolitik
						has_completed_focus = AET_archonate_help
					}
				}
			}
		}
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus AET_anarchy"
		add_political_power = -100
		country_event = { id = greifwald.76 }
		hidden_effect = { #collapse focus tree
				load_focus_tree = {
					tree = greifwald_anarchy_focus
					keep_completed = yes
				}
				mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
			}
	}
	search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_MANPOWER FOCUS_FILTER_STABILITY FOCUS_FILTER_POLITICAL }
}

					is_in_home_area = yes

						owner = {

								free_building_slots = {
									building = arms_factory
									size > 0

								}

				level = 1
				instant_build = yes
			}
		}
		add_offsite_building = {
			type = arms_factory
			level = 2
		}
		remove_state_core = 495
		if = {
			limit = {

	x = -1
	y = 4
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 100
	}
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus AET_neutral_factories"
		add_political_power = -50
		random_owned_controlled_state = {
			limit = {
				free_building_slots = {
					building = industrial_complex
					size > 0
					include_locked = yes
				}
				OR = {
					is_in_home_area = yes
					NOT = {
						owner = {
							any_owned_state = {
								free_building_slots = {
									building = industrial_complex
									size > 0
									include_locked = yes
								}
								is_in_home_area = yes
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
			add_building_construction = {
				type = industrial_complex
				level = 1
				instant_build = yes
			}
		}
		random_owned_controlled_state = {
			limit = {
				free_building_slots = {
					building = industrial_complex
					size > 0
					include_locked = yes
				}

shared_focus = {
	id = AET_archonate_help
	icon = GFX_focus_generic_diplomatic_treaty
	cost = 5.00
	#prerequisite = { focus = AET_start_focus }
	mutually_exclusive = { focus = AET_realpolitik }
	mutually_exclusive = { focus = AET_anarchy }
	x = 40
	y = 0
	offset = {
			x = -18
			y = 0
			trigger = {
				has_completed_focus = AET_archonate_help
			}
		}
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 200
	}
	allow_branch = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = obsolete_focus_branches_visibility
						option = HIDE
					}
				}
				NOT = {
					OR = {
						has_completed_focus = AET_anarchy
						has_completed_focus = AET_realpolitik
					}
				}
			}
		}
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus AET_archonate_help"
		decrease_poverty = yes
		custom_effect_tooltip = AET_poverty_removal
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = greifwald.21 days = 60 } country_event = { id = greifwald.64 } country_event = { id = greifwald.65 days = 130 } }
		hidden_effect = { #collapse focus tree
			load_focus_tree = {
				tree = greifwald_spooky_focus
				keep_completed = yes
			}
			mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
		}
	}
}

shared_focus = {
	id = AET_flame_tanks
	icon = GFX_focus_tartan_factory
	cost = 4
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 100
	}
	relative_position_id = AET_army_1
	x = -3
	y = 1
	prerequisite = { focus = AET_army_1 }
	prerequisite = { focus = AET_wave_one focus = AET_anarchic_army focus = AET_maarmy }
	available = {
		HEL = {
			exists = no
		}
	}
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus AET_flame_tanks"
		##the original idea was to dump a few hundred flame tanks on the player and say "figure it out", but in between when this focus was added and when the nation was released, flame tanks were turned from a tech into a special project
		set_technology = { gwtank_chassis = 1 }
		if = {
			limit = { has_dlc = "No Step Back" }
			create_equipment_variant = {
				name = "Ordained Cannons"
				type = light_tank_artillery_chassis_0
				parent_version = 0
				modules = {
					main_armament_slot = tank_medium_howitzer
					turret_type_slot = tank_light_fixed_superstructure_turret
					suspension_type_slot = tank_bogie_suspension
					armor_type_slot = tank_riveted_armor
					engine_type_slot = tank_gasoline_engine
					special_type_slot_1 = extra_ammo_storage
					special_type_slot_2 = extra_ammo_storage
					special_type_slot_3 = extra_ammo_storage
					special_type_slot_4 = extra_ammo_storage
				}
				upgrades = {
					tank_nsb_engine_upgrade = 4
					tank_nsb_armor_upgrade = 0
				}
				icon = "gfx/interface/technologies/armour_folder/WNG_imp_light_tank.dds"
			}
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
				type = light_tank_artillery_chassis
				amount = 15
				producer = AET
				variant_name = "Ordained Cannons"
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
				type = light_tank_artillery_chassis
				amount = 15
				producer = AET
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_completed_focus = AET_archonate_help
			}
			495 = {
				add_building_construction = {
					type = magical_facility
					level = 1
					instant_build = yes
					province = 10549
				}
			}
			add_breakthrough_points = {
				specialization = specialization_magical
				value = 1
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_completed_focus = AET_anarchy
			}
			495 = {
				add_building_construction = {
					type = nuclear_facility
					level = 1
					instant_build = yes
					province = 10549
				}
			}
			add_breakthrough_points = {
				specialization = specialization_nuclear
				value = 1
			}
		}
		else = {
			495 = {
				add_building_construction = {
					type = air_facility
					level = 1
					instant_build = yes
					province = 10549
				}
			}
			add_breakthrough_points = {
				specialization = specialization_air
				value = 1
			}
		}
	}
	search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_ARMY_BONUS }
}
